data-pitch-placement-id="«R1ar7d7mskunb»" data-pitch-placement="keypoints_pitch" data-testid="pitch-container-keypoints_pitch"></div></div></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="mx-[24px] h-[1px] border-b-[1px] border-gray-200 from-transparent to-gray-200 pt-[16px] md:-mx-[40px] md:h-[16px] md:border-b-0 md:bg-gradient-to-b md:pt-0"></div><!--/$--></section><section class="mx-auto bg-white px-6 pt-9 sm:pt-4 md:pt-4 md:pb-8 lg:px-10"><div class="mx-auto md:max-w-[880px] lg:max-w-[1280px]"><div class="foolcom-grid-content-sidebar mt-9"><div><div id="article-body" class="article-body"><p>In contrast to the mainstream artificial intelligence (AI) sector, which is dominated by a host of well-known large and megacap players, in the quantum computing space, the most popular stocks so far include a small collection of relatively unknown companies. One that has emerged as a perceived leader in the <a href="https://www.fool.com/investing/stock-market/market-sectors/information-technology/ai-stocks/quantum-computing-stocks/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">quantum computing space</a> is <strong>IonQ</strong> <span class="ticker-mention inline-flex items-center font-bold" data-id="369917">(<a href="/quote/nyse/ionq/" class="font-bold hover:underline">IONQ</a> <span class="ml-1 text-red-900">2.10%</span>)</span>.</p>
<p>With shares up more than 30% over the last year, IonQ stock has outperformed both the <strong>S&amp;P 500</strong> and <strong>Nasdaq Composite</strong>. Yet Wall Street thinks IonQ&#x27;s rally is just getting started. The average price target among analysts covering IonQ is $65 --  more than 100% higher than current trading levels.</p>
<p>While it&#x27;s tempting to follow the hype, I think Wall Street is wrong on this one.</p>
<div class="image"><img alt="Researchers in a lab experimenting on a quantum computer." loading="lazy" width="880" height="464" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="h-auto max-w-full rounded object-contain" style="color:transparent" sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 880px" srcSet="https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=320&amp;op=resize 320w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=384&amp;op=resize 384w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=640&amp;op=resize 640w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=750&amp;op=resize 750w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=828&amp;op=resize 828w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=1080&amp;op=resize 1080w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;op=resize 1200w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=1920&amp;op=resize 1920w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=2048&amp;op=resize 2048w, https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=3840&amp;op=resize 3840w" src="https://g.foolcdn.com/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fg.foolcdn.com%2Feditorial%2Fimages%2F860325%2Fgettyimages-2211414345-4.jpg&amp;w=3840&amp;op=resize"/>
<p class="caption">Image source: Getty Images.</p>
</div>
<h2 class="my-6 text-2xl font-bold">IonQ&#x27;s explosive revenue growth is less meaningful than it seems</h2>
<p>Last year, IonQ reported jaw-dropping 202% revenue growth to $130 million. Similarly impressive is the company&#x27;s guidance for 2026: Management forecasts revenue to be in the range of $225 to $245 million, representing 81% growth at the midpoint.</p><div class="my-8 lg:hidden"><div id="foolcom_sidebar_top_container" class="pitch-container" data-pitch-placement-id="«R8mbrd7mskunb»" data-pitch-placement="foolcom_sidebar_top" data-testid="pitch-container-foolcom_sidebar_top"></div></div>
<p>With integrations with each of the big three cloud service providers -- <strong>Microsoft</strong> Azure, <strong>Amazon</strong> Web Services, and Google Cloud Platform -- in addition to a strategic partnership with <strong>Nvidia</strong>, you probably think that IonQ&#x27;s approach to building a <a href="https://www.fool.com/terms/v/vertically-integrated/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">vertically integrated</a> quantum computing ecosystem is poised for explosive AI-driven growth over the next several years.</p><div class="mb-8 flex justify-center"></div>
<p>Here is why I&#x27;m not impressed by IonQ&#x27;s growth arc: The company has spent more than <a href="https://www.fool.com/investing/2026/02/11/where-will-ionq-stock-be-in-1-year/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">$4 billion on acquisitions</a> over the last couple of years. So not only is a major portion of IonQ&#x27;s revenue -- and its revenue growth -- coming from inorganic (acquired) assets, the company has yet to generate much from these sources relative to what it paid.</p><div><div id="in_line_article_pitch_container" class="pitch-container" data-pitch-placement-id="«Roubrd7mskunb»" data-pitch-placement="in_line_article_pitch" data-testid="pitch-container-in_line_article_pitch"></div></div>
<section class="shadow-card mb-[40px] border border-gray-300"><div class="flex flex-wrap place-content-between"><div class="flex w-full place-items-center lg:w-3/4"><div class="p-[8px] text-center" <h2 class="my-6 text-2xl font-bold">IonQ has a money problem that the market isn&#x27;t paying attention to ... yet</h2>
<p>While IonQ has crossed the $100 million sales milestone, the company is burning cash like there&#x27;s no tomorrow. In 2025, IonQ posted net losses of over $500 million, and its operating cash flow was negative $283 million. The company is nowhere close to becoming profitable. </p>
<p>Moreover, with this type of cash burn rate, IonQ&#x27;s liquidity of $2.4 billion doesn&#x27;t give it much of a runway. This raises the question: How is IonQ even funding its growth?</p>
<p><a href="https://ycharts.com/companies/IONQ/chart/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img alt="IONQ Shares Outstanding Chart" loading="lazy" width="720" height="441" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="h-auto max-w-full rounded object-contain" style="color:transparent;max-width:720px" sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 720px" srcSet="https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 320w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 384w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 640w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 750w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 828w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 1080w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 1200w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 1920w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 2048w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png 3840w" src="https://media.ycharts.com/charts/6b8d78b74e7c53e0630ea6881aa49cd6.png"/></a></p>
<p class="caption"><a href="https://ycharts.com/companies/IONQ/shares_outstanding" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">IONQ Shares Outstanding</a> data by <a href="https://ycharts.com" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">YCharts.</a></p>
<p>Since 2024, IonQ&#x27;s <a href="https://www.fool.com/terms/o/outstanding-shares/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">outstanding share</a> count has almost doubled. Notice that significant issuances occurred throughout the last year -- while the stock price was soaring.</p>
<p>The premise here is that IonQ has taken advantage of its rising valuation by issuing stock to raise money and pad its balance sheet. Management then used that capital to fund acquisitions that it marketed as game-changing growth catalysts -- further fueling the hype cycle.</p>
<h2 class="my-6 text-2xl font-bold">Why IonQ could lose 80% of its value by year&#x27;s end</h2>
<p>Issuing stock to fund growth and diluting shareholders in the process is not a sustainable strategy. I think it&#x27;s only a matter of time before investors catch on to IonQ&#x27;s playbook and rotate their capital toward more durable opportunities in the tech landscape.</p>
<p>In my view, IonQ trades more like a <a href="https://www.fool.com/investing/stock-market/types-of-stocks/meme-stocks/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">meme stock</a> than a sound investment. While the company continues to promote a narrative that echoes those that were once common among dot-com bubble darlings, I predict that IonQ stock will crater in a similar fashion to <strong>Cisco</strong> in the early 2000s.</p>
<p><a href="https://ycharts.com/companies/CSCO/chart/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img alt="CSCO Market Cap Chart" loading="lazy" width="720" height="441" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="h-auto max-w-full rounded object-contain" style="color:transparent;max-width:720px" sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 720px" srcSet="https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 320w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 384w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 640w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 750w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 828w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 1080w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 1200w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 1920w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 2048w, https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png 3840w" src="https://media.ycharts.com/charts/e4c3f222c632ba82417616a0ed41c7f8.png"/></a></p>
<p class="caption"><a href="https://ycharts.com/companies/CSCO/market_cap" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">CSCO Market Cap</a> data by <a href="https://ycharts.com" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">YCharts</a></p>
<p>By year&#x27;s end, I think it&#x27;s more likely that IonQ will be trading below $10 than it is to double and hit Wall Street&#x27;s target.</p></div><div class="mb-12"><div id="article-pitch" Previously, Adam was an investment banking analyst specializing in mergers and acquisitions, as well as debt and equity capital raises, for software companies. He later worked in corporate development at venture-backed technology start-ups. He holds a bachelor’s degree in business administration with a concentration in finance from the University of Richmond.</div><div class="mt-5 items-center sm:flex"><a class="mr-6 text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-900" href="/author/20479/"><span class="font-medium">TMFmoneyball</span></a><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><svg class="h-5 w-5 text-black" viewBox="0 0 50 50" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="false" role="img"><title>X</title><path d="M 11 4 C 7.134 4 4 7.134 4 11 L 4 39 C 4 42.866 7.134 46 11 46 L 39 46 C 42.866 46 46 42.866 46 39 L 46 11 C 46 7.134 42.866 4 39 4 L 11 4 z M 13.085938 13 L 21.023438 13 L 26.660156 21.009766 L 33.5 13 L 36 13 L 27.789062 22.613281 L 37.914062 37 L 29.978516 37 L 23.4375 27.707031 L 15.5 37 L 13 37 L 22.308594 26.103516 L 13.085938 13 z M 16.914062 15 L 31.021484 35 L 34.085938 35 L 19.978516 15 L 16.914062 15 z"></path></svg><a class="font-medium text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-900" href="https://x.com/moneyballinvest" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">@<!-- -->moneyballinvest</a></div></div></div></div></section><footer class="mt-8 mb-12 border-t pt-4 text-sm text-gray-600"><div class="[&amp;_h4]:text-primary-500 max-w-none [&amp;_h4]:text-lg [&amp;_h4]:font-bold [&amp;_ol]:list-decimal [&amp;_ol]:pl-9 [&amp;_ul]:list-disc [&amp;_ul]:space-y-2 [&amp;_ul]:pl-4"><p><em><a href="https://www.fool.com/author/20479/" class="text-cyan-900 hover:text-cyan-800">Adam Spatacco</a> has positions in Amazon, Microsoft, and Nvidia.
